### [1] [Ethics of Care for Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16303)
*Alexander Serebrenik,Sebastian Baltes*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文认为软件工程研究对工业实践影响有限的原因在于研究者只"关心"抽象概念而非具体实践者，主张采用关怀伦理来改善这一状况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件工程研究对工业实践的影响往往有限，研究者虽然声称关心工业影响和实践者，但通常停留在抽象层面，未能真正关怀具体情境中的个体实践者。

Method: 采用关怀伦理的哲学框架，分析软件工程研究中"关心"与"关怀"的区别，提出将关怀伦理应用于软件工程研究的理论立场。

Result: 识别出软件工程研究中"关心工业影响"（抽象概念）与"关怀具体实践者"（具体个体）之间的对立，这是研究影响有限的关键原因。

Conclusion: 主张在软件工程研究中采用关怀伦理，并讨论了这一转变对研究者和会议组织者的具体影响和启示。

Abstract: Software engineering researchers repeatedly argue that the impact of their research on industrial practice, while desired and intended, is rarely achieved. We believe that a possible explanation of this phenomenon is the opposition of "caring about" and "caring for", based on the ethics of care. Indeed, while software engineering is collaborative and hence builds on interpersonal relations, researchers tend to care about "industrial impact" and "practitioners" in abstract terms, but rarely care for specific individuals working in specific contexts facing specific challenges. In this position paper, we advocate for the adoption of ethics of care in software engineering and discuss the implications of this adoption for researchers and conference organizers.

</details>


### [2] [Results-Actionability Gap: Understanding How Practitioners Evaluate LLM Products in the Wild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16304)
*Willem van der Maden,Malak Sadek,Ziang Xiao,Aske Mottelson,Q. Vera Liao,Jichen Zhu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究团队通过访谈19位从业者，识别出LLM产品评估的10种实践，包括从非正式的"氛围检查"到组织元工作，并提出了"结果可操作性差距"这一新挑战及解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着组织将大型语言模型集成到数字产品中，其不可预测性使传统评估方法失效，但从业者如何应对这一挑战尚不清楚。

Method: 通过对19位来自不同行业的从业者进行访谈，识别出10种评估实践，并分析成功团队的模式。

Result: 除了确认4个已有挑战外，提出了第5个新挑战"结果可操作性差距"（从业者收集评估数据但无法转化为具体改进），并提供了弥合这一差距的策略。

Conclusion: 这些解释性实践是对LLM特性的必要适应而非方法学失败，HCI研究者应支持从业者系统化现有实践而非开发新评估框架。

Abstract: How do product teams evaluate LLM-powered products? As organizations integrate large language models (LLMs) into digital products, their unpredictable nature makes traditional evaluation approaches inadequate, yet little is known about how practitioners navigate this challenge. Through interviews with nineteen practitioners across diverse sectors, we identify ten evaluation practices spanning informal 'vibe checks' to organizational meta-work. Beyond confirming four documented challenges, we introduce a novel fifth we call the results-actionability gap, in which practitioners gather evaluation data but cannot translate findings into concrete improvements. Drawing on patterns from successful teams, we contribute strategies to bridge this gap, supporting practitioners' formalization journey from ad-hoc interpretive practices (e.g., vibe checks) toward systematic evaluation. Our analysis suggests these interpretive practices are necessary adaptations to LLM characteristics rather than methodological failures. For HCI researchers, this presents a research opportunity to support practitioners in systematizing emerging practices rather than developing new evaluation frameworks.

</details>


### [3] [Rethinking Artifact Evaluation for Software Engineering in the Age of Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16306)
*Christoph Treude,Christopher M. Poskitt,Rashina Hoda*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 论文主张将软件工程研究中的工件评估提升为同行评审的一等公民，以应对生成式AI降低叙事质量作为严谨性信号的有效性，并更有效地分配评审注意力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI大幅降低了撰写高质量研究叙事的成本，使得评审者可能过度关注写作质量和文献定位等相对容易改进的方面，而忽视了评估论文的科学实质。同时，评估方法实现正确性、分析严谨性和证据支持性仍然需要大量人力和专业知识。

Method: 采用立场论文的形式，将同行评审视为注意力分配问题，分析生成式AI如何削弱叙事质量作为严谨性信号的有效性，并论证工件评估应该在同行评审决策中发挥更重要的作用。

Result: 论文提出在软件工程研究中，科学实质主要体现在代码、数据、证据和分析样本、实验基础设施等工件中。通过将工件评估作为同行评审的核心组成部分，可以更有效地分配评审注意力，确保评审聚焦于研究的科学价值而非表面叙事质量。

Conclusion: 在生成式AI时代，软件工程研究应该将工件评估提升为同行评审的一等公民，这有助于评审者更有效地分配注意力，确保评审决策基于研究的科学实质而非表面叙事质量，从而提高评审质量和研究严谨性。

Abstract: Peer review in software engineering research operates under tight time constraints, while generative AI has substantially reduced the human effort required to produce polished research narratives. Reviewer attention is often spent on aspects of submissions such as writing quality or literature positioning that have become relatively less effort-intensive to address, rather than on evaluating the scientific substance of a paper. At the same time, assessing whether methods are implemented correctly, analyses are sound, and claims are supported by evidence remains effort-intensive and dependent on human expertise. In software engineering research, this substance is frequently embodied in artifacts, including code, data, evidence and analysis samples, and experimental infrastructure. In this position paper, we argue that artifact evaluation should be treated as a first-class component of peer review. We frame peer review as an attention allocation problem, examine how generative AI weakens narrative quality as a signal of rigor, and argue that artifact evaluation should play a more prominent role in peer review decisions.

</details>


### [4] [AgentGuard: A Multi-Agent Framework for Robust Package Confusion Detection via Hybrid Search and Metadata-Content Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16309)
*Yu Li,Wei Ma,Zhi Chen,Ye Liu,Lingxiao Jiang,Junyi Tao,Hao Liu,Yongqiang Lyu,Qiang Hu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AgentGuard是一个基于多智能体的框架，用于检测软件包混淆攻击，通过混合相似性搜索和融合机器学习模型显著提高了检测精度并降低了误报率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源软件的普及使软件供应链成为Package Confusion攻击的主要目标，现有检测方法存在单信号检索策略、高误报率和易受对抗性规避等局限性，无法有效区分命名相似但代码不同的良性包和恶意包。

Method: AgentGuard采用多智能体框架：首先使用微调的词嵌入模型和混合相似性搜索发现潜在混淆目标，然后通过融合机器学习模型评估风险，该模型结合了多维元数据组和创新的包内容分析组。

Result: 在ConfuDB和NeupaneDB数据集上的评估显示，AgentGuard显著优于现有最佳方法ConfuGuard和Typomind，精度提高了12%-49%，同时将误报率降低了11%-35%，并能有效发现混淆包。

Conclusion: AgentGuard通过多智能体框架和融合分析方法有效解决了现有软件包混淆检测方法的局限性，在保持高检测率的同时显著降低了误报率，为开源软件供应链安全提供了更可靠的保护。

Abstract: The proliferation of open-source software (OSS) has made software supply chains prime targets for attacks like Package Confusion, where adversaries publish malicious packages with names deceptively similar to legitimate ones. To protect against such attacks and safeguard the use of OSS, multiple confusion detection methods have been proposed. However, existing methods are limited to single-signal retrieval strategies (relying solely on lexical or semantic metrics), struggle with high false positive rates (FPR), and are vulnerable to adversarial evasion. Critically, as content-agnostic approaches, they fundamentally fail to distinguish benign packages with high naming similarity from malicious, code-dissimilar impersonations, leading to persistent high FPR. To address these limitations, we introduce AgentGuard, a novel multi-agents based framework for package confusion detection. Specifically, it first discovers potential confusion targets using fine-tuned word embedding models with hybrid similarity search. After that, It subsequently evaluates risk via a fused machine learning model that uniquely combines: (1) a multi-dimensional metadata group and (2) a novel package content analysis group, to reduce the FPR and mitigate the impact of adversarial evasion. To assess the effectiveness of AgentGuard, we evaluate it on challenging ConfuDB and NeupaneDB datasets. Our results demonstrate that AgentGuard significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, ConfuGuard and Typomind, improving precision by 12\%-49\% while simultaneously reducing the FPR by 11\%-35\%, and effectively discovers the confused package.

</details>


### [5] [Software Self-Extension with SelfEvolve: an Agentic Architecture for Runtime Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16314)
*Md Asif Iqbal Fahim,Oluwadamilola Adebayo,Alessio Ferrari*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SelfEvolve：一种基于LLM的自主代码生成架构，使系统能够在运行时自我扩展新功能，超越传统自适应系统


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自适应系统只能重新配置现有组件，无法生成全新功能模块。LLM的代码生成能力为实现系统自我进化提供了可能，使系统能在运行时自主扩展能力

Method: 提出SelfEvolve架构，采用编排的智能体管道，支持运行时自我扩展——基于用户请求自主生成和集成新功能，无需系统重启或开发者干预

Result: 在11个自我扩展任务中平均Pass@1达到92.7%（51/55），显著优于AutoGen、MetaGPT和AgentCoder等基线方法，比最佳基线AutoGen提升61.8%且有统计显著性

Conclusion: 证明了通过自主代码生成实现运行时能力扩展的可行性，为系统自主进化以满足用户需求的新范式提供了初步证据，为个性化、自我改进的系统铺平道路

Abstract: Traditional self-adaptive systems automatically reconfigure existing components in response to changing requirements, but provide limited support for the generation of novel functionalities. The software generation capabilities of large language models (LLMs) open the possibility to create entirely new modules at runtime, enabling a form of self-evolution beyond traditional self-adaptation. We present SelfEvolve, an orchestrated agentic pipeline architecture enabling runtime self-extension--the autonomous addition of new capabilities during execution--as a preliminary form of self-evolution. Self-extension focuses on the autonomous generation and integration of new functions, based on user requests, without requiring a system restart or developer intervention. Evaluation of our architecture across 11 self-extension tasks demonstrates an average Pass@1 of 92.7% (51/55), outperforming developer-focused code generation baselines like AutoGen, MetaGPT, and AgentCoder. SelfEvolve achieves 61.8% improvement over the best baseline, i.e. Autogen, with statistical significance. This work demonstrates the feasibility of runtime capability extension through autonomous code generation. This provides preliminary evidence for a paradigm in which systems autonomously evolve to satisfy user needs, paving the way towards individualised, self-improving systems.

</details>


### [6] [Be a Partner, not a Bystander in Software Engineering Practice: Bridging the Gaps between Academia and Industry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16315)
*Mohammad Masudur Rahman,Mehil B. Shah*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该立场论文主张重新审视软件工程学术界与工业界的关系，通过实证调查发现SE社区对其研究影响力和行业相关性深感担忧，并提出改革行动呼吁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI重大突破（如LLMs）和软件行业大规模采用AI，需要重新审视学术界与SE行业的关系。软件工程社区对其研究影响力和行业实践相关性深感担忧，需要通过实证研究来验证这一立场。

Method: 通过收集软件工程社区的调查响应进行实证研究，分析社区对研究影响力和行业相关性的看法，基于调查结果提出改革建议。

Result: 研究提供了支持作者立场的令人信服的证据，表明软件工程社区确实对其研究影响力和行业实践相关性存在深切担忧。

Conclusion: 需要新的行动呼吁和软件工程领域的改革，以重新构想软件工程社区的未来，维持学术界与工业界之间的共生关系。

Abstract: Software engineering conferences bring together thousands of academicians and software practitioners so that academic research and professional practices can influence each other. In essence, a symbiotic relationship exists between the research community and the software industry, which must be maintained, nurtured and re-examined periodically. Given the major AI breakthroughs (e.g., LLMs) and large-scale adoption of AI by the software industry, a re-examination of the relationship between academia and the SE industry is highly warranted. In this position paper, we argue that the software engineering community is deeply concerned about its research impact and relevance to industry practices. By conducting an empirical study using the survey responses from the SE community, we not only provide compelling evidence supporting our position but also propose new calls for action and reforms in SE, and thus envision a new future for the software engineering community.

</details>


### [7] [Software-Defined Vehicle Ecosystems in Transformation -- A Systematic Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16319)
*Heidi Hietala,Nirnaya Tripathi,Prabhash Rathnayake,Yueqiang Xu,Tero Päivärinta,Ella Peltonen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究分析了软件定义汽车（SDV）生态系统，识别了6个合作层级、12个利益相关者群体、5个权威维度，以及软件开发、组织、行业市场、法规伦理等方面的挑战和机遇，提出了多层次SDV生态系统模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 汽车行业正从硬件为中心转向软件定义车辆（SDV），软件复杂性增加使得传统的企业中心化开发模式不足，需要生态系统协作。然而，目前对SDV生态系统如何形成和运作的理解仍然不足。

Method: 通过文献研究，识别SDV生态系统的协作结构、利益相关者、角色和权威关系，分析面临的挑战和机遇，构建多层次SDV生态系统模型。

Result: 识别了6个合作层级涉及12个利益相关者群体，受5个权威维度影响；面临6个核心软件开发挑战，以及组织、行业市场、法规伦理方面的挑战；同时存在软件开发、组织、行业市场、公共价值等方面的机遇。

Conclusion: 将SDV重新定位为多层次社会技术生态系统，软件是核心结构原则但不是唯一决定因素；开发了整合利益相关者、协作结构和治理的多层次SDV生态系统模型，为未来研究和实践提供方向。

Abstract: The automotive industry is shifting from hardware-centric development toward software-defined vehicles (SDVs), where software drives functionality, value creation, and competitive differentiation. Growing software complexity renders firm-centric and proprietary software development models insufficient, prompting a shift toward ecosystem collaboration among OEMs, suppliers, and software firms. Yet, how these SDV ecosystems emerge and operate in response to software-driven development remains insufficiently understood. This study enhances our understanding of SDV ecosystems, outlines their collaborative structures, identifies stakeholders, their roles and authority, and highlights associated challenges and opportunities. This study identifies six levels of collaboration involving twelve stakeholder groups shaping SDV ecosystem transformation. These collaborations are influenced by five dimensions of authority. SDV ecosystems face six core software development challenges alongside six organisational, six industry and market, and four regulatory, legal, and ethical challenges. The literature also highlights five key software development opportunities complemented by six organisational, four industry and market, and two public value and ethical opportunities. SDV ecosystem research is primarily technical, concentrating on architectures and standardisation, while lacking studies on governance and collaborative software business models that reflect regional characteristics and power dynamics. We reposition SDVs as multi-level socio-technical ecosystems where software functions as the core structuring principle but does not alone determine ecosystem success. We develop a multi-level SDV ecosystem model, integrating stakeholders, collaborative structures, and governance across ecosystem levels, and outline directions for future research and practice.

</details>


### [8] [How Robustly do LLMs Understand Execution Semantics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16320)
*Claudio Spiess,Prem Devanbu,Earl T. Barr*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLMs在代码理解任务中表现出显著差异：开源推理模型在代码变换和输入扰动下保持相对稳定（准确率38%-67%），而GPT-5.2虽然原始基准得分接近完美（99%），但在扰动下准确率下降20-24%，显示出脆弱性。所有模型在预测引发异常的扰动输入时表现更差，且性能取决于异常类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLMs是否使用内部世界模型还是依赖复杂模式匹配，通过代码理解的鲁棒性来探究。使用程序输出预测任务作为测试框架，考察模型在代码变换和输入扰动下的表现差异。

Method: 使用标准的程序输出预测任务（CRUXEval基准），对代码进行变换和输入扰动，测试不同LLMs的响应。特别关注模型在预测引发异常的扰动输入时的表现，并研究异常类型对预测性能的影响。同时探索了改善异常预测能力的补救措施。

Result: 开源推理模型（DeepSeek-R1系列）在扰动下保持相对稳定的准确率（38%-67%），而GPT-5.2虽然原始基准得分高达99%，但在扰动下准确率下降20-24%。所有模型在预测引发异常的扰动输入时表现显著更差，且性能受异常类型影响。补救措施对改善异常预测能力有一定效果。

Conclusion: 所有模型在代码理解方式上存在局限性，GPT-5.2等前沿模型虽然原始性能优异，但鲁棒性不足。使用扰动评估代码模型具有重要价值，揭示了模型可能更多依赖模式匹配而非真正的理解。异常预测是评估代码理解能力的关键维度。

Abstract: LLMs demonstrate remarkable reasoning capabilities, yet whether they utilize internal world models or rely on sophisticated pattern matching remains open. We study LLMs through the lens of robustness of their code understanding using a standard program-output prediction task. Our results reveal a stark divergence in model behavior: while open-source reasoning models (DeepSeek-R1 family) maintain stable, albeit somewhat lower accuracies (38% to 67%) under code transformations & input perturbations, the frontier model GPT-5.2 exhibits significant brittleness. Despite achieving a near-perfect score of 99% on the original, unperturbed CRUXEval benchmark, perturbed inputs trigger accuracy declines between 20% and 24%. In addition, we find that many models perform much worse at predicting behavior on perturbed inputs that raise exceptions, and that prediction performance depends on the kind of exception. We study remedies to address this deficiency in exception prediction, and evaluate the effect of these remedies on the ability to predict non-exception behaviors. Our findings both point to limitations in the way all models understand code, and establish the value of using perturbation to evaluate code models.

</details>


### [9] [LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems for Code Generation: A Multi-Vocal Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16321)
*Zeeshan Rasheeda,Muhammad Waseema,Kai-Kristian Kemella,Mika Saari,Pekka Abrahamsson*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过多源文献综述方法，系统分析了基于LLM的多智能体系统在代码生成领域的研究现状，涵盖114项研究，总结了采用动机、模型配置、挑战解决方案及未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于LLM的多智能体系统在代码生成领域的研究和工业应用日益增长，但缺乏对学术和工业来源证据的系统性综合，无法全面把握该领域的研究现状。

Method: 采用多源文献综述方法，结合学术和工业来源，包括同行评审研究和灰色文献，系统性地综合分析了114项相关研究。

Result: 1) 识别出采用多智能体系统进行代码生成的九类动机；2) 系统分析了研究中使用的模型和评估基准；3) 将报告挑战和相应解决方案综合为6个主类和26个子类；4) 识别出未来研究方向，组织为6个主类和18个子类。

Conclusion: 该多源文献综述为研究者和从业者提供了系统性的知识框架，有助于推动进一步研究并支持多智能体系统在工业环境中的实际应用。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled multi-agent systems to perform autonomous code generation for complex tasks. Despite the recent growth in research and industrial applications in this area, there is little work on synthesizing evidence from both academic and industrial sources to capture the current state of research on LLM-based multi-agent systems for code generation. To this end, we conducted a Multi-Vocal Literature Review (MLR), combining insights from both academia and industry, including peer-reviewed studies and grey literature. The aim of this study is to systematically synthesize and analyze existing knowledge on LLM-based multi-agent systems for code generation. Specifically, the review examines the motivations for their use, employed benchmarks and models, key challenges, proposed solutions, and potential directions for future research.
  We selected and reviewed 114 studies, and the key findings are: 1) the identified reasons for adopting multi-agent systems for code generation were classified into nine categories; 2) the models and evaluation benchmarks utilized across the studies were systematically analyzed to provide a structured overview of commonly adopted LLM configurations and assessment practices; 3) the reported challenges and corresponding solutions were synthesized into six main categories and 26 subcategories; and 4) future research directions were identified and organized into six main categories and 18 subcategories. The results of this MLR will assist researchers and practitioners in pursuing further studies and supporting the real-world adoption of multi-agent systems in industrial settings.

</details>


### [10] [Steerable Instruction Following Coding Data Synthesis with Actor-Parametric Schema Co-Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16322)
*Tinglin Huang,Bo Chen,Xiao Zhang,Kai Shen,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: IFCodeEvolve是一个用于生成指令配对编程数据的框架，通过参数化函数模式库和蒙特卡洛树搜索采样器，结合演员模型与模式库协同进化，显著提升基础模型性能，32B模型达到与专有SOTA模型相当的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在自动编程中理解和遵循人类指令的能力至关重要，但大规模指令配对编程数据的合成仍然未被充分探索，特别是在确保多个约束之间的逻辑兼容性方面具有挑战性。

Method: 提出IFCodeEvolve框架：1) 将指令表示为参数化函数模式，通过动态约束实例化构建覆盖广泛指令空间的模式库；2) 应用蒙特卡洛树搜索采样器高效导航该空间，使用演员模型反馈作为动态终止信号；3) 引入协同进化范式，基于采样器统计通过模式组合和变异迭代推进演员模型和模式库。

Result: IFCodeEvolve显著提升了基础模型性能，其32B模型达到了与专有SOTA模型相当的水平。同时贡献了IFCodeBench基准，这是一个包含解决方案和基于AST的鲁棒验证的全面人工验证基准。

Conclusion: IFCodeEvolve通过演员-模式协同进化框架有效解决了指令配对编程数据生成的挑战，为自动编程中的指令遵循能力提供了有效的解决方案，并通过IFCodeBench基准为领域评估提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Interpreting and following human instructions is a critical capability of large language models (LLMs) in automatic programming. However, synthesizing large-scale instruction-paired coding data remains largely unexplored and is particularly challenging when ensuring logical compatibility among multiple constraints. In this study, we propose IFCodeEvolve, an actor-schema co-evolution framework for instruction following coding data generation. By representing instructions as parametric function schema, we construct a library that covers the vast instruction space via dynamic constraint instantiation. Building upon this, Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) sampler is applied to efficiently navigate this space, utilizing actor model feedback as a dynamic termination signal. Furthermore, to progressively explore challenging problems, we introduce a co-evolving paradigm that iteratively advances both the actor model and the schema library, via schema composition and mutation, based on sampler statistics. Empirical results demonstrate that IFCodeEvolve significantly boosts base model performance, with our 32B model achieving parity with proprietary SOTA models. Additionally, we contribute IFCodeBench, a comprehensive human-verified benchmark equipped with solutions and robust AST-based verification.

</details>

Following a structured search and manual screening protocol, we completed literature collection in November 2025 and identified 145 unique papers across seven logging tasks. We synthesize the research area through a unified, task-driven taxonomy, summarize common design patterns (prompting/ICL, retrieval grounding, fine-tuning, tool/agent augmentation, and verification), and analyze evaluation practices, datasets, metrics, and reproducibility. ### [14] [How Do Developers Interact with AI? An Exploratory Study on Modeling Developer Programming Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16393)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合方法研究，将76名开发者分为AI辅助组和非AI组，让他们完成编程任务（Python API管理或Java SQL）。通过屏幕录制、自我报告意图、工具支持行动、情绪标注，并结合调查问卷和访谈进行数据分析。

Result: 提出了S-IASE四维模型来描述编程行为：特定开发状态下的意图、行动、支持工具和情感。分析显示聚合和顺序行为模式：AI辅助开发者更专注于主动创建代码、评估和验证生成结果；AI辅助组情绪更稳定，而非AI组情绪波动更大；访谈还发现一些开发者有冒名顶替感，对依赖AI感到内疚或自我怀疑。

Conclusion: 该研究填补了理解开发者-AI交互复杂性的重要空白，提出的S-IASE模型为更全面地分析编程行为提供了框架，揭示了AI辅助对开发者认知和情感状态的多方面影响。

Abstract: Artificial Intelligence (AI) is reshaping how developers adopt software engineering practices, yet the multi-dimensional nature of developer-AI interaction remains under-explored. Prior studies have primarily examined dimensions observable from developer activities such as "Prompt crafting" and "Code Editing", overlooking how hidden intentions and emotional dimensions intertwine with concrete actions during AI-assisted programming. To understand this phenomenon, we conducted a mixed-methods study with 76 developers split into AI-assisted and non-AI groups. Each performed programming tasks (Python with API management or Java with SQL). Developers retrospectively labeled their self-reported intentions, tool-supported actions, and emotions from screen recordings, supplemented by surveys and interviews. Our user study resulted in a novel model named S-IASE with four dimensions to describe programming behavior: intention, action, supporting tool, and emotion for a given development state. Our analysis reveals aggregated and sequential behavioral patterns. For example, using AI assistants often makes developers more focused on actively creating code, evaluating, and verifying generated results. AI-assisted participants showed emotionally stable development flow, as opposed to non-AI-assisted participants who experienced more fluctuating emotions. Interviews revealed further nuance: some developers reported impostor-like feelings, expressing guilt or self-doubt about relying on AI. Our work bridges an important gap in understanding the complexities of developer-AI interaction in programming context.

Still, to this day, no secondary study has mapped the research landscape of how commit messages have been used in corrective software maintenance. We present a systematic mapping study of 97 primary sources published between 2004 and May 2025, where we examine the goals, potential utilization of source code artifacts along with commit messages, methodologies, stakeholders, and the key findings about their influence on corrective maintenance. Our analysis reveals a growing interest in the usage of commit messages to perform corrective maintenance tasks, in particular for bug analysis and bug fix identification goals. Surprisingly few studies address other themes such as automated program repair, security development practices, etc. We find that the software artifacts most used in combination with commit messages are commit "diffs" and that repository mining, together with natural language processing (NLP) and artificial intelligence/machine learning (AI/ML) are the methodological foundations of studies in this field. Among stakeholders considered in previous studies, developers play the most important role in shaping corrective maintenance practices. Key findings in previous studies about commit messages establish their significant role in corrective maintenance, due to the fact that they carry crucial information helpful for stakeholders to understand and improve the code base through the software evolution process. ### [17] [SpecPylot: Python Specification Generation using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16560)
*Ragib Shahariar Ayon,Shibbir Ahmed*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SpecPylot使用LLM生成候选合约，通过crosshair的符号执行进行验证。当发现具体反例时，工具会更新生成的合约而不修改程序本身。还能生成覆盖率驱动的pytest存根并保留详细的执行工件用于调试。

Result: 评估表明SpecPylot能为大多数程序生成crosshair兼容的合约，但也揭示了有限符号探索和LLM行为差异带来的实际限制。

Abstract: Automatically generating formal specifications could reduce the effort needed to improve program correctness, but in practice, this is still challenging. Many developers avoid writing contracts by hand, which limits the use of automated verification tools. Recent large language models (LLMs) can generate specifications from code, but these specifications often fail in terms of verification. The reason is syntax errors, overly strict constraints, or mismatches with program behavior. We present SpecPylot, a Python tool that synthesizes executable specifications for Python programs as icontract annotations and checks them using crosshair's symbolic execution. The tool relies on LLMs to propose candidate contracts and uses crosshair to validate them. When crosshair finds a concrete counterexample, SpecPylot updates only the generated contracts and leaves the program itself untouched. In addition, the tool can produce coverage-driven pytest stubs and keep detailed execution artifacts that are useful during debugging. Overall, the evaluation indicates that SpecPylot is able to generate crosshair-compatible contracts for most programs, but it also highlights the practical limits introduced by bounded symbolic exploration and differences in LLM behavior.

### [18] [Certified Program Synthesis with a Multi-Modal Verifier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16584)
*Yueyang Feng,Dipesh Kafle,Vladimir Gladshtein,Vitaly Kurin,George Pîrlea,Qiyuan Zhao,Peter Müller,Ilya Sergey*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LeetProof是一个基于多模态验证器Velvet的认证程序合成系统，通过结合动态验证、自动证明和交互式证明脚本，解决了现有认证合成方法中规范质量差和验证工具碎片化的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 认证程序合成面临两大挑战：1) 从自然语言生成的规范要么太弱无意义，要么太强无法实现，现有方法缺乏系统检测这些缺陷的手段；2) 程序验证工具碎片化，每种工具只支持特定推理模式（自动激活或交互式），限制了合成方法能处理的任务范围。

Method: LeetProof围绕多模态验证器Velvet构建认证合成工作流，Velvet嵌入在Lean中，结合了动态验证、自动证明和交互式证明脚本。系统通过随机化基于属性的测试在代码合成前验证生成的规范，根据验证条件将合成任务分解为子问题，并将剩余证明义务委托给专门用于Lean的前沿AI证明器。

Result: 在从先前认证合成工作中提取的基准测试上，LeetProof的规范验证发现了现有参考基准中的缺陷，其分阶段流水线在相同预算下实现了比单模态基线显著更高的完全认证解决方案率，在两个前沿LLM后端上表现一致。

Conclusion: 多模态验证器为认证程序合成提供了系统化的规范验证和灵活的证明策略，LeetProof展示了这种方法的有效性，能够处理更广泛的合成任务并提高认证成功率。

Abstract: Certified program synthesis (aka vericoding) is the process of automatically generating a program, its formal specification, and a machine-checkable proof of their alignment from a natural-language description. Two challenges make vericoding difficult. First, specifications synthesised from natural language are often either too weak to be meaningful or too strong to be implementable, yet existing approaches lack systematic means to detect such defects. Second, the landscape of program verifiers is fragmented: each tool supports a particular reasoning mode -- auto-active (e.g., Dafny, Verus) or interactive (e.g., Coq, Lean) -- with its own trade-off between automation and expressivity. This forces every synthesis methodology to be tailored to a single verification paradigm, limiting the class of tasks it can handle effectively.
  We overcome both challenges by structuring the certified synthesis workflow around a multi-modal verifier -- a single tool combining dynamic validation, automated proofs, and interactive proof scripting in one foundational framework. We realise this idea in LeetProof, an agentic pipeline built on Velvet, a multi-modal verifier embedded in Lean. Multi-modality enables LeetProof to validate generated specifications via randomised property-based testing before any code is synthesised, decompose the synthesis task into sub-problems guided by verification conditions, and delegate residual proof obligations to frontier AI provers specialised for Lean. We evaluate LeetProof on benchmarks derived from prior work on certified synthesis. Our specification validation uncovers defects in existing reference benchmarks, and LeetProof's staged pipeline achieves a significantly higher rate of fully certified solutions than a single-mode baseline at the same budget -- consistently across two frontier LLM backends.

</details>


### [19] [AI Slop and the Software Commons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16754)
*Sebastian Baltes,Marc Cheong,Christoph Treude*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AI生成的"垃圾内容"在软件领域造成了公地悲剧，个人生产力提升的成本被外部化到审查能力、代码库完整性、公共知识资源等方面，需要系统性解决方案


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在揭示AI生成内容（AI slop）在软件开发中造成的系统性风险，即个人生产力提升带来的成本外部化问题，这类似于"公地悲剧"现象，需要集体行动来解决

Method: 采用公地悲剧理论框架，分析AI生成内容对软件开发生态系统的负面影响，并基于奥斯特罗姆的公共资源治理原则提出具体解决方案

Result: 识别出AI slop导致的多重成本外部化问题：审查能力负担、代码库完整性受损、公共知识资源污染、协作信任破坏和人才管道问题

Conclusion: 需要工具开发者、团队领导和教育者采取具体行动，基于奥斯特罗姆的公共资源治理原则建立可持续的治理机制，而不是依赖个人自律

Abstract: In this article, we argue that AI slop in software is creating a tragedy of the commons. Individual productivity gains from AI-generated content externalize costs onto reviewer capacity, codebase integrity, public knowledge resources, collaborative trust, and the talent pipeline. AI slop is cheap to generate and expensive to review, and the review layer is already thin. Commons problems are not solved by individual restraint. We outline concrete next steps for tool developers, team leads, and educators, grounded in Ostrom's design principles for enduring commons institutions.

### [20] [Mitigating Prompt-Induced Cognitive Biases in General-Purpose AI for Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16756)
*Francesco Sovrano,Gabriele Dominici,Alberto Bacchelli*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文研究了提示诱导的认知偏见对通用人工智能在软件工程决策支持中的影响，开发了PROBE-SWE基准测试，发现现有提示工程技术无法显著减少偏见敏感性，提出了一种基于最佳实践和公理推理的新方法，将偏见敏感性平均降低51%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在软件工程决策支持中，问题陈述和需求通常使用自然语言描述，微小的措辞变化（如流行度暗示或结果揭示）可能导致通用人工智能模型做出次优决策。研究旨在了解提示诱导的认知偏见如何影响AI决策，并开发有效的缓解策略。

Method: 1. 开发PROBE-SWE动态基准测试，配对有偏见和无偏见的相同软件工程困境版本，控制逻辑和难度，针对八种软件工程相关偏见；2. 测试常见提示工程技术（如思维链、自我去偏见）的有效性；3. 提出基于Prolog风格推理过程的新方法，通过引出最佳实践和注入公理推理线索来减少偏见敏感性。

Result: 1. 常见提示工程技术在单个偏见基础上没有统计学上显著的减少效果；2. 提出的新方法（引出最佳实践+公理推理线索注入）将总体偏见敏感性平均降低51%（p < .001）；3. 通过主题分析发现了与高度偏见敏感性相关的语言模式。

Conclusion: 提示诱导的认知偏见是软件工程决策支持中通用人工智能系统的实际问题。现有提示工程技术不足以缓解偏见敏感性，而基于引出软件工程最佳实践和公理推理的方法能显著减少偏见。研究结果为识别高风险使用场景和未来对策开发提供了指导。

Abstract: Prompt-induced cognitive biases are changes in a general-purpose AI (GPAI) system's decisions caused solely by biased wording in the input (e.g., framing, anchors), not task logic. In software engineering (SE) decision support (where problem statements and requirements are natural language) small phrasing shifts (e.g., popularity hints or outcome reveals) can push GPAI models toward suboptimal decisions. We study this with PROBE-SWE, a dynamic benchmark for SE that pairs biased and unbiased versions of the same SE dilemmas, controls for logic and difficulty, and targets eight SE-relevant biases (anchoring, availability, bandwagon, confirmation, framing, hindsight, hyperbolic discounting, overconfidence). We ask whether prompt engineering mitigates bias sensitivity in practice, focusing on actionable techniques that practitioners can apply off-the-shelf in real environments. Testing common strategies (e.g., chain-of-thought, self-debiasing) on cost-effective GPAI systems, we find no statistically significant reductions in bias sensitivity on a per-bias basis. We then adopt a Prolog-style view of the reasoning process: solving SE dilemmas requires making explicit any background axioms and inference assumptions (i.e., SE best practices) that are usually implicit in the prompt. So, we hypothesize that bias-inducing features short-circuit assumptions elicitation, pushing GPAI models toward biased shortcuts. Building on this, we introduce an end-to-end method that elicits best practices and injects axiomatic reasoning cues into the prompt before answering, reducing overall bias sensitivity by 51% on average (p < .001). Finally, we report a thematic analysis that surfaces linguistic patterns associated with heightened bias sensitivity, clarifying when GPAI use is less advisable for SE decision support and where to focus future countermeasures.

*Aakash Sorathiya,Gouri Ginde*

TL;DR: 该论文对2012年以来关于从应用商店评论中分析用户伦理关切（隐私、安全、可访问性等非功能性需求）的研究进行了系统综述，涵盖37项相关研究，提出了研究议程并指出开发者和研究人员可如何利用这些发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动应用中的隐私、安全、可访问性等伦理关切通常通过应用商店评论表达，但这些评论混杂在用户体验、问题报告和新功能讨论中，难以识别。虽然过去十年有大量研究从应用评论中提取有价值信息，但缺乏对伦理关切分析研究的系统综述。

Method: 采用系统综述方法，从初始的553项研究中通过特定纳入和排除标准筛选出37项相关研究（2012年以来）。分析内容包括研究目标、方法、策略以及使用的额外资源（如应用隐私政策）。研究覆盖的评论数量从500到6.26亿条，应用数量从单个到130万个。

Result: 研究发现用户评论中持续存在的障碍包括隐私、安全、可访问性、透明度、公平性、问责制和安全性问题。研究目标、方法和策略呈现多样性，研究人员通常结合应用隐私政策等额外资源来分析伦理关切。

Conclusion: 该综述提出了一个研究议程，重点关注四个关键领域，包括伦理关切相关应用评论的自动提取和分类。调查结果可帮助开发者和系统架构师在开发生命周期早期识别和优先处理非功能性需求，研究人员可在此基础上开发自动检测伦理关切的工具。

Abstract: Privacy, security, and accessibility, like ethical concerns in mobile applications (a.k.a. apps), commonly subsumed under non-functional requirements, are generally reported by users through app reviews available in app stores. However, these remain unidentified among other types of reviews, such as user experiences, problem reports, and new feature discussions. Over the past decade, extensive research has focused on extracting valuable information from app reviews, including feature requests and bug reports. However, there remains a lack of a synthesis of research related to app review analysis for exploring users' ethical concerns. This paper presents a comprehensive survey of this research area, covering 37 relevant studies published since 2012, identified from the initial 553 studies using specific inclusion and exclusion criteria. The studies examined vary in review counts, ranging from 500 to 626 million, and include between a single and 1.3 million apps. Our detailed analysis highlights diverse objectives, methodologies, and strategies, along with additional resources such as app privacy policies, which researchers generally utilize to analyze ethical concerns. Our findings also identify persistent barriers to privacy, security, accessibility, transparency, fairness, accountability, and safety, as reported by users in app reviews. Furthermore, we propose a research agenda that focuses on four key areas, including automated extraction and classification of ethical concerns-related app reviews. Our survey outcomes can assist developers and system architects in recognizing and prioritizing non-functional requirements at the initial stages of the development lifecycle, whereas researchers can expand upon this synthesis to create tools for the automated detection of ethical concerns.

### [22] [Bias in the Loop: Auditing LLM-as-a-Judge for Software Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16790)
*Zixiao Zhao,Amirreza Esmaeili,Fatemeh Fard*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLM作为代码评估法官存在显著的提示偏见敏感性，即使代码片段不变，微小提示修改也能显著改变评估结果，威胁代码评估的有效性和可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM越来越多地被用作代码评估的法官，特别是在人类评审或测试覆盖不足的情况下，当前实践缺乏对可靠性和偏见的系统分析。重复评估可能不一致，微小提示修改可能导致结果波动，语义等价的扰动可能引发分歧判决。

Method: 通过测量优先的视角研究LLM作为代码法官。分析代码生成、代码修复和测试生成三个任务中的点式评估机制，系统探究提示诱导的偏见。研究考虑重复运行的难度级别和受控提示干预，每次隔离一个呈现线索，使用一致性和偏见敏感性评估法官性能。

Result: 法官决策对提示偏见高度敏感，即使底层代码片段不变。在所有三个任务中，多个偏见系统性地将偏好转向提示偏好的选项：当该选项与正确答案一致时提高准确性，否则显著降低准确性。在某些情况下，这些效应大到足以改变任务级结论和模型相对排名。

Conclusion: 报告的法官性能可能反映提示伪影而非稳定的评估能力，这对代码评估的有效性和可复现性构成直接威胁。因此，LLM作为法官的研究应同时报告偏见敏感性和准确性，并纳入显式控制以支持软件工程中更可信的模型比较。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly used as judges to evaluate code artifacts when exhaustive human review or executable test coverage is unavailable. LLM-judge is increasingly relevant in agentic software engineering workflows, where it can help rank candidate solutions and guide patch selection. While attractive for scale, current practice lacks a principled account of reliability and bias: repeated evaluations of the same case can disagree; small prompt edits can swing outcomes; and seemingly semantics-preserving, human-equivalent perturbations may elicit divergent verdicts. This paper studies LLM-as-a-Judge for code through a measurement-first lens. We analyze two pointwise judging regimes across code generation, code repair task, and test generation, and we systematically probe prompt-induced biases. Our study considers difficulty levels for repeated runs and controlled prompt interventions that isolate one presentation cue at a time, and it evaluates judges using consistency and sensitivity to bias. We find that judge decisions are highly sensitive to prompt biases even when the underlying code snippet is unchanged. Across all three tasks, several biases systematically shift preferences toward the option favored by the prompt, improving accuracy when that option aligns with the gold answer but substantially reducing it otherwise. In some settings, these effects are large enough to change task-level conclusions and alter relative model rankings. These findings show that reported judge performance may reflect prompt artifacts rather than stable assessment ability, posing a direct threat to the validity and reproducibility of code evaluation. We therefore argue that LLM-as-a-Judge studies should report bias sensitivity alongside accuracy and incorporate explicit controls to support more trustworthy model comparison in software engineering.

### [23] [Gleaner: A Semantically-Rich and Efficient Online Sampler for Microservice Diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16810)
*Yifan Yang,Aoyang FANG,Songhan Zhang,Pinjia He*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Gleaner是一个在线尾部采样框架，通过将trace表示为"bag-of-edges"并采用集合操作，解决了传统基于图分析的采样方法性能瓶颈问题，显著提升了采样效率和RCA准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务分布式追踪产生海量数据需要智能采样，但现有基于图分析的尾部采样方法计算开销大，无法在线使用，需要在采样保真度和性能之间做出权衡。

Method: Gleaner将每个trace表示为增强日志语义的"bag-of-edges"，用高效的集合操作替代缓慢的图算法，并采用告警驱动的配额和多样性保持策略来优先采样异常和罕见trace。

Result: Gleaner处理每个trace仅需0.74ms，相比基线方法，Trace Pattern Coverage提升达128.7%，Shannon Entropy提升达32.9%。在仅1%采样率下，RCA准确性比次优采样器提升42%-107%，甚至比使用完整未采样数据集更准确。

Conclusion: Gleaner打破了采样保真度与性能的权衡，将智能采样从数据缩减技术重新定义为自动化运维的强大信号增强范式，其采样数据比完整数据集更能提升RCA准确性。

Abstract: Distributed tracing in microservices is critical for diagnostics but generates overwhelming data volumes, necessitating intelligent sampling. To maximize fidelity, state-of-the-art (SOTA) tail-based samplers analyze complete (or even log-enriched) traces by modeling them as graphs. However, this reliance on computationally expensive graph analysis creates a performance bottleneck that prohibits their use in online settings.
  To this end, we propose Gleaner, an online tail-sampling framework that breaks this trade-off. It is founded on the key insight that explicit graph structures are unnecessary for high-fidelity trace grouping. Instead, Gleaner represents each trace as a "bag-of-edges" augmented with log semantics, replacing slow graph algorithms with highly efficient set-based operations. It also employs an alarm-driven quota and a diversity-preserving strategy to prioritize anomalous and rare traces for downstream Root Cause Analysis (RCA). Experimentally, Gleaner processes traces at 0.74ms each, improving Trace Pattern Coverage by up to 128.7% and Shannon Entropy by up to 32.9% over baselines. At just a 1% sampling rate, Gleaner improves RCA accuracy by 42%-107% over the next-best sampler. Moreover, RCA on Gleaner's sampled data is more accurate than with the entire, unsampled dataset. This result reframes intelligent sampling from a data reduction technique to a powerful signal enhancement paradigm for automated operations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前开发实践中存在行为版本控制的缺失：开发者常用Git版本控制源代码，但很少持久化和查询运行时行为在不同版本间的演化。这导致软件演化分析和CI中存在盲点，丰富的执行信息被丢弃，通常简化为通过/失败结果，忽略了部分测试预言、测试不稳定性、静默输出或性能漂移等问题。

Method: 提出行为协同版本控制范式，将Git历史与行为档案耦合。行为档案是一个可追加、可查询的存储库，存储测试运行期间收集的选定运行时观察（如方法I/O和性能信号），按提交和测试上下文进行索引。基于代码/测试/行为指纹构建最小数据模型和变更诊断，并通过笔记本电脑规模的原型系统验证可行性，该系统重放Python项目的历史提交，在本地Parquet支持的存储中归档运行时观察，并检测文本差异不明显的行为变化。

Conclusion: 行为协同版本控制通过将Git历史与运行时行为档案耦合，实现了语义差异分析、行为感知的回归定位和追溯审计，补充了主动的、信号特定的监控工具，为软件演化分析提供了更全面的视角。

Abstract: Behavioral Co-Versioning remains absent from mainstream practice: while developers routinely version source code with Git, they rarely persist and query how run-time behavior evolves across revisions. This paper argues that this mismatch contributes to a blind spot in software evolution analysis and CI, where rich execution information is discarded and typically reduced to pass/fail outcomes -- despite partial test oracles, flakiness, and silent output or performance drift. We propose \textit{Behavioral Co-Versioning}, a paradigm that couples the Git history with a \textit{Behavioral Archive}: an append-only, queryable store of selected run-time observations (e.g., method I/O and performance signals) collected during test runs and keyed by commit and test context. This enables semantic diffing, behavior-aware regression localization, and retrospective auditing by querying historical executions, complementing proactive, signal-specific monitoring tools. We first outline a minimal data model and change diagnostics based on code/test/behavior fingerprints, and then demonstrate feasibility with a laptop-scale prototype that replays historical commits of a Python project, archives run-time observations in a local Parquet-backed store, and detects behavioral changes not apparent from textual diffs.

Abstract: We present MEMRES, an agentic system for Python dependency resolution that introduces a multi-level confidence cascade where the LLM serves as the last resort. On HG2.9K using Gemma-2 9B (10 GB VRAM). MEMRES resolves 2503 of 2890 (86.6%, 10-run average) snippets, combining intra-session memory with our confidence cascade for the remainder. ### [26] [HELO-APR: Enhancing Low-Resource Program Repair through Cross-Lingual Knowledge Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17016)
*Zhipeng Wang,Boyang Yang,Yidong Wan,Liuye Guo,You Lv,Tao Zheng,Zhuowei Wang,Tieke He*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: HELO-APR是一个两阶段自动程序修复框架，通过从高资源编程语言向低资源编程语言进行跨语言知识迁移，解决了LLMs在低资源语言上修复效果差的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在高资源编程语言的自动程序修复上表现良好，但在低资源编程语言上效果显著下降，主要原因是缺乏足够的经过验证的错误-修复对用于训练。

Method: HELO-APR采用两阶段框架：1）通过从高资源语言的错误-修复对合成高质量的低资源语言训练数据，保持缺陷类型一致性并确保代码符合语言习惯；2）采用课程学习策略，逐步进行高资源语言修复学习、跨语言修复对齐和低资源语言修复适应。

Result: 实验表明，在xCodeEval基准测试中，HELO-APR显著优于基线方法，将DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B的Pass@1从31.32%提升到48.65%，CodeLlama-7B从1.67%提升到11.97%，同时将CodeLlama的平均目标编译率从49.77%提高到91.98%。在Defects4Ruby上，BLEU-4从61.20提升到66.79，ROUGE-1从76.76提升到83.59。

Conclusion: 经过验证的跨语言监督为改进低资源语言中基于LLM的修复提供了一个可重复使用的方法，HELO-APR框架有效解决了低资源编程语言自动程序修复的挑战。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) perform well on automatic program repair (APR) for high-resource programming languages (HRPLs), but their effectiveness drops sharply in low-resource programming languages (LRPLs), due to a lack of sufficient verified buggy-fixed pairs for APR training. To address this challenge, we propose HELO-APR (High-resource Enabled LOw-resource APR), a two-stage APR framework that enables cross-lingual transfer of repair knowledge from HRPLs to LRPLs. HELO-APR (1) constructs high-quality LRPL training data by synthesizing LRPL buggy-fixed pairs from HRPL counterparts, preserving defect type consistency while ensuring the synthesized code is idiomatic, and then (2) adopts a curriculum learning strategy that progressively performs HRPL repair learning, cross-lingual repair alignment, and LRPL repair adaptation, improving repair effectiveness in LRPLs. Using C++ as the source HRPL and Ruby and Rust as the target LRPLs, experiments on xCodeEval show that HELO-APR consistently outperforms strong baselines, increasing Pass@1 from 31.32% to 48.65% on DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B and from 1.67% to 11.97% on CodeLlama-7B, while improving syntactic validity by raising the average target compilation rate on CodeLlama from 49.77% to 91.98%. On Defects4Ruby, HELO-APR increases BLEU-4 from 61.20 to 66.79 and ROUGE-1 from 76.76 to 83.59 on CodeLlama-7B, indicating higher similarity to developer patches in real-world settings. Finally, we conduct ablation studies to assess the necessity of each core component. These results suggest that verified cross-lingual supervision provides a reusable approach for improving LLM-based repair in low-resource languages.

### [27] [AI Observability for Developer Productivity Tools: Bridging Cost Awareness and Code Quality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17092)

### [28] [Layer-wise MoE Routing Locality under Shared-Prefix Code Generation: Token-Identity Decomposition and Compile-Equivalent Fork Redundancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17182)
*Shun-ichiro Hayashi,Daichi Mukunoki,Tetsuya Hoshino,Takahiro Katagiri*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究Qwen3.5-35B-A3B-FP8模型在代码生成中MoE专家路由的重叠模式，发现相同token位置的路由相似度远高于不同token位置，中间层呈现特殊交叉模式，树搜索生成的代码高度集中在少数汇编等价组中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在LLM代码生成中，多个候选代码通常从同一提示并行生成（如best-of-N采样或多候选代码补全），这些请求可以通过公共前缀共享KV缓存，但它们的MoE专家路由重叠程度以及这种重叠在不同层间的变化尚未得到充分理解。

Method: 使用Qwen3.5-35B-A3B-FP8模型（256个路由专家，top-8），通过基于树搜索的分支生成从共享前缀生成851个完整代码（温度0.7），并使用基于编译器输出的对齐方法（gcc -S -O0汇编）分析结果，控制token身份混淆。

Result: 1. 相同token位置Jaccard相似度达0.649（40倍随机），不同token位置相似度为0.175（11倍随机）。2. 层间分解显示交叉模式：相同token路由相似度在所有层都高于不同token，但在中间层（L14-20）下降，而不同token相似度在中间层达到峰值（14倍随机）。3. 树搜索代码生成中，67%成功编译的代码集中在top-3汇编等价组，99.6%组内差异为注释和空行。

Conclusion: 研究通过层间分解细化了先前工作的"上下文无关路由"主张，表明top-P搜索（包括束搜索）中的多样性构成重大挑战，为改进LLM代码生成中的搜索效率提供了机会。

Abstract: In LLM-based code generation, multiple code candidates are often generated in parallel from the same prompt -- for example, in best-of-N sampling or multi-candidate code completion. These requests can share KV caches through a common prefix, yet the extent to which their Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) expert routing overlaps, and how this overlap varies across layers, remains insufficiently understood. We study Qwen3.5-35B-A3B-FP8 (256 routed experts, top-8) by performing tree-search-based branching generation from a shared prefix (851 completed codes, temperature 0.7) and analyzing the results with a compiler-output-based alignment (gcc -S -O0 assembly) that controls for token-identity confounds. Our findings are threefold: (1) At positions where both sequences generated the same token, Jaccard similarity reaches 0.649 (40x random), while even at positions with different tokens it remains 0.175 (11x random). (2) A layer-wise decomposition reveals a crossing pattern: same-token routing similarity exceeds different-token similarity across all layers, but dips in the middle layers (L14-20), while different-token similarity peaks in the middle layers at 14x random. (3) In tree-search code generation, 67% of successfully compiled codes concentrate in the top three assembly-equivalent groups, and 99.6% of within-group differences consist of comments and blank lines. We show that diversity in top-P search, including beam search, poses a significant challenge. These results refine the "context-independent routing" claim of prior work through layer-wise decomposition and suggest opportunities for improving search efficiency in LLM code generation.

### [30] [React-ing to Grace Hopper 200: Five Open-Weights Coding Models, One React Native App, One GH200, One Weekend](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17187)
*Alex Potanin*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 评估5个开源代码模型在React Native应用生成任务上的表现，发现SWE-Bench排名不能预测实际任务性能，Kimi-K2.5在3位量化下表现最佳，同时揭示了推理模型部署中的三个新发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估当前最先进的开源代码语言模型在实际多文件React Native应用生成任务上的性能，探索模型量化、硬件成本与性能之间的关系，并识别现有评估基准与实际部署需求之间的差距。

Method: 在NVIDIA GH200 576GB硬件上，对5个开源代码模型（Kimi-K2.5、GLM-5.1、Qwen3-Coder-480B、DeepSeek-V3.2）进行单任务评估。任务要求生成包含认证、用户每日计数和Web兼容性的React Native应用，评估标准包括项目能否开箱即用和功能正确性。

Result: Kimi-K2.5在激进的3位量化（UD-Q3_K_XL，480GB）下产生了最完整且符合规范的输出，超越了SWE-Bench Pro分数更高的模型。研究还发现：1）默认temperature=0会导致推理模型架构采样卡顿；2）推理模型的思考痕迹可能通过文件路径解析器泄露；3）所有模型都存在原生移动API到Web平台适配的训练数据缺口。

Conclusion: SWE-Bench排名不能准确预测实际代码生成任务性能；推理模型部署存在特殊挑战；效率派架构（10-15B活跃参数）能以约1/7的硬件成本达到与规模派（32-40B活跃参数）相当的SWE-Bench结果；所有模型在跨平台API适配方面存在训练数据不足的问题。

Abstract: We evaluate five state-of-the-art open-weights coding language models -- Kimi-K2.5 (at Q3 and Q4 quantizations), GLM-5.1, Qwen3-Coder-480B, and DeepSeek-V3.2 -- on a single multi-file React Native application generation task on NVIDIA GH200 576 GB hardware. The task specifies authentication, per-user per-day counting, and web compatibility, and is evaluated on whether the generated project runs out-of-the-box and on feature-level correctness. We find that SWE-Bench rankings do not predict task performance: Kimi-K2.5 at aggressive 3-bit quantization (UD-Q3_K_XL, 480 GB) produces the most complete and specification-compliant output, outranking models with substantially higher SWE-Bench Pro scores. We document three novel deployment findings: (1) default temperature=0 in coding tools causes sampling hangs with reasoning-model architectures, (2) reasoning-model thinking traces can leak through integration tools' file-path parsers, and (3) web-platform adaptation of native-mobile APIs is a universal training-data gap across every model tested. We also map the hardware-tier structure of April 2026 open-weights coding models, identifying two architectural schools and showing that the efficiency school (10-15 B active parameters) delivers equivalent SWE-Bench results at roughly 1/7th the hardware cost of the scale school (32-40 B active parameters).

We also compare their performance when prompted with a) Source code, b) PlantUML representation of source code, and c) Text-based descriptions of the source code. We investigate the detection of five design patterns: singleton, adapter, bridge, composite and decorator. Our preliminary results indicate that LLMs show promise for automatically detecting design patterns, with NextCoder and Gemma 3 demonstrating comparatively higher accuracy than other models evaluated, and the ensemble approaches enhancing the overall efficiency of design pattern detection. ### [33] [Isolating Recurring Execution-Dependent Abnormal Patterns on NISQ Quantum Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17519)
*Zhenyu Qi,Qian Zhang,Haotang Li,Sen He,Jiyuan Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: QRisk框架通过发现硬件特定的异常模式来改进量子编译，使用delta调试技术识别噪声模型未预测的电路片段，并通过交换可交换门来破坏这些模式，从而减少实际硬件噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前量子编译器依赖校准得到的噪声模型来指导电路映射和优化，但这些模型独立表征门和量子位错误，忽略了上下文相关效应（如串扰和相关调度错误），导致两个在噪声模型下评分相同的编译电路在实际硬件上表现差异很大，且编译器无法从这种反复出现的不匹配中学习。

Method: QRisk使用delta调试技术从实际硬件执行中隔离出紧凑的电路片段，这些片段持续产生噪声模型未预测的额外错误；然后验证这些模式在重复运行和校准窗口中的持久性；验证后的模式存储在特定后端的模式数据库中；编译时，QRisk扫描编译后的电路寻找已知模式的出现，并应用有针对性的可交换门交换来破坏这些模式，产生语义等效但异常模式更少的电路。

Result: 在两个IBM后端（ibm_fez和ibm_marrakesh）上使用Grover搜索电路进行评估，发现这些模式在数月的多个校准窗口中持续存在；通过可交换门交换破坏这些模式，在ibm_fez上减少了24%的额外硬件噪声（Spearman ρ = 0.515, p = 0.0007），在ibm_marrakesh上减少了45%（ρ = 0.711, p < 0.0001），而噪声模型预测所有等效电路的误差相同；在第三个后端上的测试确认这些模式是后端特定的。

Conclusion: QRisk框架能够发现后端特定的异常模式，并通过有针对性的电路变换有效减少实际硬件噪声，为量子编译器提供了从硬件执行中学习并改进电路质量的新机制。

Abstract: Quantum compilers rely on calibration-derived noise models to guide circuit mapping and optimization. These models characterize gate and qubit errors independently and miss context-dependent effects such as crosstalk and correlated scheduling errors. As a result, two compiled circuits that score equally under the noise model can behave very differently on real hardware, and the compiler has no mechanism to learn from such recurring mismatches.
  We present QRisk, a framework that discovers backend-specific abnormal patterns from real hardware executions. QRisk uses delta debugging to isolate compact circuit fragments that consistently produce excess error not predicted by the noise model, then validates their persistence across repeated runs and calibration windows. The verified patterns are stored in a backend-specific pattern database. At compilation time, QRisk scans a compiled circuit for occurrences of known patterns and applies targeted commuting gate swaps to disrupt them, producing a semantically equivalent circuit with fewer abnormal patterns.
  We evaluate QRisk on two IBM backends (ibm_fez and ibm_marrakesh) using Grover search circuits. On both backends, discovered patterns persist across multiple calibration windows over months. Disrupting these patterns via commuting gate swaps reduces excess hardware noise by 24% on ibm_fez (Spearman $ρ$ = 0.515, p = 0.0007) and 45% on ibm_marrakesh ($ρ$ = 0.711, p < 0.0001), while the noise model predicts identical error for all equivalent circuits. Testing on a third backend confirms that these patterns are backend-specific.

</details>


### [34] [Single-Language Evidence Is Insufficient for Automated Logging: A Multilingual Benchmark and Empirical Study with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17529)
*Renyi Zhong,Yichen Li,Yulun Wu,Jinxi Kuang,Yintong Huo,Michael R. Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MultiLogBench是一个多语言日志生成基准测试，包含6种编程语言的63,965个代码实例和744个维护历史案例，用于评估LLM在日志生成各环节的性能，发现跨语言差异显著，需要多语言评估来获得可靠结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化日志生成研究主要基于Java语言的仓库快照数据集，不清楚模型行为和选择是否能在不同编程语言生态系统和实际代码演化中泛化。需要建立多语言基准来验证自动化日志生成的鲁棒性。

Method: 创建MultiLogBench基准，包含6种编程语言的63,965个生产代码仓库快照实例、744个开发者在维护中引入日志的修订历史案例，以及用于鲁棒性分析的配对转换修订历史分支。使用7个当代大语言模型在统一协议下评估日志站点定位、框架锚点匹配、严重性预测、消息生成、变量恢复和级联整体质量。

Result: 结果显示明显的跨语言差异：框架锚点匹配是最语言敏感的组件，循环和嵌套可调用站点是最难的结构上下文，模型排名仅在顶级保持稳定。这些模式在修订历史数据中大致保持，而转换输入不会导致广泛的同向性能崩溃。

Conclusion: 关于自动化日志生成的鲁棒性声明需要多语言评估和维护导向的验证。MultiLogBench展示了跨语言差异的重要性，为未来研究提供了更全面的评估框架。

Abstract: Logging statements are central to debugging, failure diagnosis, and production observability, yet writing them requires developers to decide where to place a logging statement, which API and severity level to use, and what runtime information to expose. Automated logging aims to reduce this burden, but existing evidence remains dominated by Java-centric repository-snapshot dataset. It is therefore unclear whether conclusions about model behavior and model selection generalize across programming-language ecosystems or realistic code evolution. This paper presents MultiLogBench, a multilingual benchmark and empirical study spanning six programming language ecosystems. MultiLogBench contains 63,965 production-code repository-snapshot instances, 744 revision-history cases where developers introduce logging statements during maintenance, and a paired transformed revision-history branch for robustness analysis. Using seven contemporary large language models under a unified protocol, we evaluate logging-site localization, framework-anchor matching, severity prediction, message generation, variable recovery, and cascaded overall quality. Results show clear cross-language variation: framework-anchor matching is the most language-sensitive component, loop and nested-callable sites are the hardest structural contexts, and model rankings are stable only at the top tier. These patterns persist at a coarse level on revision-history data, while transformed inputs do not cause a broad same-direction performance collapse. Overall, MultiLogBench shows that robust claims about automated logging require multilingual evaluation and maintenance-oriented validation.

</details>


### [35] [AIRA: AI-Induced Risk Audit: A Structured Inspection Framework for AI-Generated Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17587)
*William M. Parris*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AI生成的代码倾向于"静默失败"——表面上功能正常但实际削弱或隐藏了保证，这可能是人类反馈优化的结果而非随机bug分布。研究提出了AIRA检测框架，发现AI生成代码的高严重性缺陷是人工代码的1.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从业者观察到AI辅助代码生成存在方向性模式：AI生成的代码倾向于静默失败，保持功能外观但削弱或隐藏保证。这可能是人类反馈优化的产物而非随机bug分布，需要系统检测框架来识别这种失败不真实模式。

Method: 提出了"奖励塑造失败假说"，定义了失败真实性概念。开发了AIRA（AI诱导风险审计）框架，包含15项确定性检查来检测代码中的失败不真实模式。进行了三项研究：企业环境审计、600文件公共语料库试点、955对955的严格匹配控制复制实验。

Result: 在最终复制实验中，AI归因文件显示每文件0.435个高严重性发现，而人工控制文件为0.242个（1.80倍）。这种效应在JavaScript、Python和TypeScript中一致，在异常处理相关模式中最为集中。结果支持AI辅助代码存在向软失败行为倾斜的方向性偏差。

Conclusion: AI生成的代码确实存在静默失败倾向，这反映了优化过程的人工反馈影响。AIRA框架适用于需要故障封闭行为的治理、合规和安全关键系统，有助于检测和防范这种风险模式。

Abstract: Practitioners have reported a directional pattern in AI-assisted code generation: AI-generated code tends to fail quietly, preserving the appearance of functionality while degrading or concealing guarantees. This paper introduces the Reward-Shaped Failure Hypothesis - the proposal that this pattern may reflect an artifact of optimization through human feedback rather than a random distribution of bugs. We define failure truthfulness as the property that a system's observable outputs accurately represent its internal success or failure state. We then present AIRA (AI-Induced Risk Audit), a deterministic 15-check inspection framework designed to detect failure-untruthful patterns in code. We report results from three studies: (1) an anonymized enterprise environment audit, (2) a balanced 600-file public corpus pilot, and (3) a strict matched-control replication comparing 955 AI-attributed files against 955 human-control files. In the final replication, AI-attributed files show 0.435 high-severity findings per file versus 0.242 in human controls (1.80x). The effect is consistent across JavaScript, Python, and TypeScript, with strongest concentration in exception-handling-related patterns. These findings are consistent with a directional skew toward fail-soft behavior in AI-assisted code. AIRA is designed for governance, compliance, and safety-critical systems where fail-closed behavior is required.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Agentic Consensus范式：1）共识层C作为主要工程制品，表示为类型属性图；2）通过同步操作Phi（实现）和Psi（再水合）保持可执行制品与C的对应关系；3）证据直接链接到C中的结构声明，使所有承诺可审计；4）将未明确说明部分量化为可测量的共识熵而非隐性猜测。

Result: 提出评估框架需超越代码正确性，转向对齐保真度、共识熵和干预距离。设计了基准任务族来衡量基于共识的工作流相比聊天驱动基线是否能减少人工干预。

Conclusion: Agentic Consensus范式通过将共识层作为主要工程制品，解决了当前AI辅助开发中的控制失败问题，使系统变更更加透明、可审计和健壮，为软件工程提供了新的评估维度。

Abstract: Vibe coding produces correct, executable code at speed, but leaves no record of the structural commitments, dependencies, or evidence behind it. Reviewers cannot determine what invariants were assumed, what changed, or why a regression occurred. This is not a generation failure but a control failure: the dominant artifact of AI-assisted development (code plus chat history) performs dimension collapse, flattening complex system topology into low-dimensional text and making systems opaque and fragile under change. We propose Agentic Consensus: a paradigm in which the consensus layer C, an operable world model represented as a typed property graph, replaces code as the primary artifact of engineering. Executable artifacts are derived from C and kept in correspondence via synchronization operators Phi (realize) and Psi (rehydrate). Evidence links directly to structural claims in C, making every commitment auditable and under-specification explicit as measurable consensus entropy rather than a silent guess. Evaluation must move beyond code correctness toward alignment fidelity, consensus entropy, and intervention distance. We propose benchmark task families designed to measure whether consensus-based workflows reduce human intervention compared to chat-driven baselines.

### [40] [When AI Models Become Dependencies: Studying the Evolution of Pre-Trained Model Reuse in Downstream Software Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17940)
*Peerachai Banyongrakkul,Mansooreh Zahedi,Christoph Treude,Haoyu Gao,Patanamon Thongtanunam*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 预训练模型（PTM）作为软件依赖项与传统软件库有本质区别：PTM变更频率更低（仅为库变更的1/3），通常在项目后期添加且会累积而非被替换，变更动机主要是能力扩展而非修复问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代软件系统越来越多地将预训练模型（PTM）作为永久依赖项，但我们对这些"PTM依赖项"如何随时间变化缺乏清晰理解。PTM具有不透明的内部结构、非标准化的快速发布周期，且开发者可将单个PTM的不同实例视为基于特定下游任务的独立功能依赖。这引发了一个关键问题：PTM是否像标准软件库一样变化，还是遵循不同的模式？

Method: 对下游PTM变更进行了首次实证研究，分析了323个GitHub开源仓库中重用开源PTM的4,988个发布版本的综合数据集。以传统软件库作为基线进行比较分析。

Result: 研究发现PTM遵循质的不同模式：1）PTM通常在项目生命周期后期添加；2）随着项目成熟，PTM倾向于累积而非被替换；3）PTM变更频率比库变更低三倍（2,814次发布过渡中仅有406次PTM变更）；4）PTM变更较少被常规记录，但更可能带有明确的理由说明；5）与库的被动演化不同，PTM演化是主动驱动的，主要由能力扩展推动，并具有独特的PTM测试不确定性记录理由。

Conclusion: PTM作为依赖项的变化模式与传统软件库有本质区别，需要重新思考在现代软件工程中如何跟踪和管理PTM依赖项。PTM的独特特性（不透明性、快速演化、多角色性质）要求新的依赖管理方法。

Abstract: Modern software systems have transitioned from purely code-based architectures to AI-integrated systems where pre-trained models (PTMs) serve as permanent dependencies. However, while the evolution of traditional software libraries is well-documented, we lack a clear understanding of how these "PTM dependencies" change over time. Unlike libraries, PTMs are characterized by opaque internals and less standardized, rapidly evolving release cycles. Furthermore, their multi-role nature enables developers to treat individual instances of a single PTM as separate functional dependencies based on their specific downstream tasks. This raises a critical question for software maintenance: do PTMs change like standard software libraries or do they follow a divergent pattern? To answer this, we present the first empirical study of downstream PTM changes, analyzing a comprehensive dataset of 4,988 releases across 323 GitHub OSS repositories that reuse open-source PTMs. Using traditional software libraries as a baseline, we find that PTMs follow a qualitatively distinct pattern. PTMs are typically added late in the project life-cycle and tend to accumulate rather than be replaced as a project matures. Our findings show that PTM changes are three times less frequent (406 of 2,814 release transitions) than library changes. PTM changes are also less routinely documented, but more likely to carry explicit rationale. Unlike libraries, which evolve reactively, PTM evolution is proactively driven by capability expansion, with a unique documented rationale of PTM testing uncertainty. Our work calls for a rethinking of how PTMs are tracked and managed as dependencies in modern software engineering.

### [41] [MASFuzzer: Fuzz Driver Generation and Adaptive Scheduling via Multidimensional API Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17977)
*Xingyu Liu,Zengqin Huang,Xiang Gao,Hailong Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MASFUZZER是一个集成多维API序列构建和自适应模糊测试调度策略的框架，用于改进软件库测试，相比现有技术提高8.54%的代码覆盖率，并发现16个未知漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统模糊测试驱动程序需要手动编写，耗时且难以覆盖复杂程序行为。现有基于LLM的自动化方法生成的驱动程序往往无法覆盖深层程序分支。

Method: MASFUZZER通过多维API序列构建和自适应调度策略改进库测试：1) 从代码库中参考API使用示例，应用基于突变传播和语义感知的API序列挖掘，合成上下文相关的API调用序列；2) 将这些多维API序列作为LLM生成有效初始驱动程序的基础；3) 采用覆盖引导的调度器优先测试最有希望的驱动程序；4) 使用驱动程序变异策略演化驱动程序。

Result: 在12个广泛使用的开源库上评估，MASFUZZER相比最先进技术实现8.54%更高的代码覆盖率，发现了16个先前未知的漏洞，其中14个被开发者确认，9个获得了CVE标识。

Conclusion: MASFUZZER为模糊测试软件库提供了一种高效实用的方法，能够系统生成模糊测试驱动程序来探索先前未测试的代码区域。

Abstract: Fuzz testing of software libraries relies on fuzz drivers to invoke library APIs. Traditionally, these drivers are written manually by developers - a process that is time-consuming and often inadequate for exercising complex program behaviors. While recent studies have explored the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) to automate fuzz driver generation, the resulting drivers often fail to cover deep program branches. To address these challenges, we propose MASFUZZER, a fuzzing framework that integrates multidimensional API sequence construction with adaptive fuzzing scheduling strategies to improve library testing. At its core, MASFUZZER synthesizes context-relevant API call sequences by referring to API usage examples from the codebase and applying mutation-propagation-based and semantic-aware API sequence mining. These multidimensional API sequences serve as the basis for LLMs to generate effective initial drivers. In addition, MASFUZZER incorporates a coverage-guided scheduler that prioritizes testing time for the most promising drivers, along with a driver mutation strategy to evolve them. This enables systematic generation of fuzz drivers to explore previously untested code regions. We evaluate MASFUZZER on 12 widely used open-source libraries. The results show that MASFUZZER achieves 8.54 percent higher code coverage than state-of-the-art techniques. Moreover, MASFUZZER uncovers 16 previously unknown vulnerabilities in extensively tested libraries, with 14 confirmed by developers and 9 assigned CVE identifiers. These results indicate that MASFUZZER provides an efficient and practical approach for fuzzing software libraries.

### [42] [CodePivot: Bootstrapping Multilingual Transpilation in LLMs via Reinforcement Learning without Parallel Corpora](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18027)
*Shangyu Li,Juyong Jiang,Meibo Ren,Sizhe Zhong,Huiri Tan,Yunhao Gou,Xu Han,Chun Yong Chong,Yun Peng,Jiasi Shen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CodePivot提出了一种利用Python作为中间表示的代码翻译训练框架，通过新颖的强化学习奖励机制，无需平行语料库即可提升多语言代码翻译能力，在10种编程语言的实验中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于训练的代码翻译方法存在两个主要问题：1）依赖成对翻译范式，难以支持多样化的编程语言，特别是低资源语言；2）强化学习奖励机制不够优化。这些问题限制了模型在低资源语言代码翻译任务上的表现。

Method: CodePivot采用Python作为中间表示（IR），通过"激进-部分-功能"奖励机制（Aggressive-Partial-Functional reward）进行强化学习训练。该框架只需在Python到其他语言的翻译任务上进行训练，就能提升多语言翻译能力，无需平行语料库。

Result: 在10种编程语言的实验中，7B参数的CodePivot模型在Python到其他语言的翻译任务上表现优异，在通用和低资源语言相关的翻译任务上均取得持续改进。它超越了参数量大数百亿的主流模型，如Deepseek-R1和Qwen3-235B-A22B-Instruct-2507，在相应任务上表现更好。

Conclusion: CodePivot通过创新的训练框架和奖励机制，有效解决了低资源语言代码翻译的挑战，无需平行语料库即可提升多语言翻译能力，为代码翻译任务提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Transpilation, or code translation, aims to convert source code from one programming language (PL) to another. It is beneficial for many downstream applications, from modernizing large legacy codebases to augmenting data for low-resource PLs. Recent large language model (LLM)-based approaches have demonstrated immense potential for code translation. Among these approaches, training-based methods are particularly important because LLMs currently do not effectively adapt to domain-specific settings that suffer from a lack of knowledge without targeted training. This limitation is evident in transpilation tasks involving low-resource PLs. However, existing training-based approaches rely on a pairwise transpilation paradigm, making it impractical to support a diverse range of PLs. This limitation is particularly prominent for low-resource PLs due to a scarcity of training data. Furthermore, these methods suffer from suboptimal reinforcement learning (RL) reward formulations. To address these limitations, we propose CodePivot, a training framework that leverages Python as an intermediate representation (IR), augmented by a novel RL reward mechanism, Aggressive-Partial-Functional reward, to bootstrap the model's multilingual transpilation ability without requiring parallel corpora. Experiments involving 10 PLs show that the resulting 7B model, trained on Python-to-Others tasks, consistently improves performance across both general and low-resource PL-related transpilation tasks. It outperforms substantially larger mainstream models with hundreds of billions more parameters, such as Deepseek-R1 and Qwen3-235B-A22B-Instruct-2507, on Python-to-Others tasks and Others-to-All tasks, respectively. In addition, it outperforms its counterpart trained directly on Any-to-Any tasks on general transpilation tasks. The code and data are available at https://github.com/lishangyu-hkust/CodePivot.

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种公平优先的设计思维方法，用于在软件架构设计中解决公平性问题，并通过研究生课程实践验证了该方法。

Motivation: 数字系统中的公平问题往往难以察觉和解决，需要系统性的方法来在软件架构设计中识别和解决公平性问题。

Method: 开发了公平优先的设计思维方法，并在研究生课程中实施，学生通过作业执行所有设计思维步骤，分析作业数据来评估方法的适用性。

Result: 提供了：(1)软件架构设计思维方法；(2)在问题和解决方案空间中处理公平性的启示；(3)教育启示。研究发现公平理论和情境识别对整体公平优先设计至关重要，建议使用复合视图处理跨领域关注点如公平性。

Conclusion: 公平优先的设计思维方法有助于在软件架构中解决公平性问题，未来将更新课程材料以提供端到端的公平可追溯性，帮助学生理解如何将公平关注转化为可操作的设计决策。

Abstract: Fairness issues often remain hidden in digital systems, making them difficult to detect and even more difficult to address. In this study, we introduce a fairness-first Design Thinking (DT) approach to support addressing fairness concerns in software architecture (SA) design. We implemented our approach in a graduate-level course where students executed all steps of our DT approach as part of an assignment. We analyzed the assignment data to reflect on the implications for applying the DT approach in SA and teaching the DT approach in SA education. As a result of this study, we provide (i) a DT approach for SA, (ii) implications of the DT approach on handling fairness in both problem and solution spaces, and (iii) implications for education. Our reflections highlight that fairness theory and context identification are essential for a holistic, fairness-first design. We propose the use of composite views to address cross-cutting concerns such as fairness. In the future, we will update the course material to provide end-to-end fairness traceability in SA, helping students to understand how fairness concerns can be translated into actionable design decisions.

### [45] [From Program Slices to Causal Clarity: Evaluating Faithful, Actionable LLM-Generated Failure Explanations via Context Partitioning and LLM-as-a-Judge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18309)
*Julius Porbeck,Christian Medeiros Adriano,Holger Giese*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了不同上下文配置对LLM生成故障解释质量的影响，发现证据丰富、故障特定的上下文能提升解释质量，而过大上下文则导致解释模糊，高质量解释与下游修复成功率正相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM调试系统生成的故障解释可能不完整或不正确，这些误导性解释对下游任务（如bug分类、修复）有害。现有工作主要将LLM生成的故障解释视为调试或修复工作流的副产品，使用通用提示处理未区分的工件，而不是将解释作为具有专门质量评估的一等输出。

Method: 系统变化调试信息以研究不同上下文组合如何影响LLM生成的故障解释质量。在真实bug上测试93种上下文配置，使用三种经济可行模型（gpt-5-mini、DeepSeek-V3.2、Grok-4.1-fast），通过六个标准评估解释，并通过用户研究验证LLM作为评判者的评分与人类评分的一致性。

Result: 解释质量受上下文组合因果影响。证据丰富、故障特定的工件能提高因果性和行动导向质量，而过大的上下文往往产生模糊解释。高质量解释与更高的下游修复通过率相关，某些模型还能生成更接近参考最小修复的补丁。低质量解释甚至可能不如无解释基线。

Conclusion: 上下文组合对LLM生成的故障解释质量有因果影响，精心设计的上下文配置能显著提升解释质量，进而改善下游修复任务表现。研究强调了将故障解释作为一等输出进行专门质量评估的重要性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based debugging systems can generate failure explanations, but these explanations may be incomplete or incorrect. Misleading explanations are harmful for downstream tasks (e.g., bug triage, bug fixing). We investigate how explanation quality is affected by various LLM context configurations. Existing work predominantly treats LLM-generated failure explanations as an ad hoc by-product of debugging or repair workflows, using generic prompting over undifferentiated artifacts such as code, tests, and error messages rather than targeting explanations as a first-class output with dedicated quality assessment. Consequently, existing approaches provide limited support for assessing whether these explanations capture the underlying fault-error-failure mechanism and for actionable next steps, and most techniques instead prioritize task success (e.g., patch correctness or review quality) over the explicit causal explanation quality. We systematically vary the debugging information to study how distinct context compositions affect the quality of LLM-generated failure explanations. Across 93 context configurations on real bugs and three economically viable models (gpt-5-mini, DeepSeek-V3.2, and Grok-4.1-fast), we evaluate explanations with six criteria and validate the LLM-as-a-judge scores against human ratings in a user study. Our results indicate that explanation quality is causally affected by context composition. Evidence-rich, failure-specific artifacts improve causal and action-oriented quality, whereas overly large contexts tend to yield vague explanations. Higher explanation-score quartiles are associated with higher downstream repair pass rates and, for some models, with fixes that are closer to the reference minimal fixes. In contrast, low-score quartiles can even underperform the no-explanation baseline. Reproduction package is publicly available.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出STAF（基于句子Transformer的可行动性过滤）方法，利用基于Transformer的架构和句子嵌入技术，将静态分析工具的发现分类为可行动和不可行动两类。

Result: 在Java项目的大型报告数据集上评估STAF，结果显示该方法能有效减少不可行动的发现数量，同时保持高准确率识别可行动问题。在项目内设置中F1分数达到89%，比现有方法至少高出11%；在跨项目设置中至少高出6%。

Abstract: Static code analysis (SCA) tools are widely used as effective ways to detect bugs and vulnerabilities in software systems. However, the reports generated by these tools often contain a large number of non-actionable findings, which can overwhelm developers to the point of ignoring them altogether -- this phenomenon is known as "alert fatigue". In this paper, we combat alert fatigue by proposing STAF: Sentence Transformer-based Actionability Filtering. Our approach leverages a transformer based architecture with sentence embeddings to classify findings into actionable and non-actionable categories. Evaluating STAF on a large dataset of reports from Java projects, we demonstrate that our method can effectively reduce the number of non-actionable findings while maintaining a high level of accuracy in identifying actionable issues. The results show that our approach can improve the usability of static analysis tools reaching an F1 score of 89%, outperforming existing methods for SCA warning filtering by at least 11% in a within-project setting and by at least 6% in a cross-project setting. By providing a more focused and relevant set of findings, we aim to enhance the overall effectiveness of static analysis in software development.

Method: 使用多模态感知框架：热成像监测头部和脚部表面温度，音频记录分析声谱特征，光流视频分析对饲养员进入的反应，环境监测记录温湿度。研究150只Lohmann LSL-Lite雏鸡，每周收集数据并提取特征。

Result: 热成像显示外周温度随年龄增加并稳定，脚部温度发育效应显著；声学特征随周龄系统性变化；光流分析显示早期对饲养员反应强烈，随年龄下降；多模态轨迹显示模态内一致性高，湿度与声学特征相关，热、声、行为域相对独立。

One hundred fifty Lohmann LSL-Lite chicks were housed across five controlled rooms; thermal and environmental data were collected system-wide, while detailed audio and video analyses focused on one representative room. Weekly aggregated features included head and foot surface temperatures, acoustic spectral descriptors, optical-flow movement responses to caretaker entry, and ambient conditions. Thermal imaging showed age-related increases and stabilization of peripheral temperatures, with foot temperature exhibiting a strong developmental effect (eta squared = 0.51). Acoustic features changed systematically across weeks (p < 0.001), consistent with vocal maturation. Optical-flow analysis revealed pronounced early reactivity to caretaker presence that declined with age (weeks 5 to 10 versus 11 to 20: t = 28.12, p = 0.00126). Z-score-normalized multimodal trajectories and correlation analysis (false discovery rate q < 0.05) showed strong within-modality consistency (r = 0.85 to 0.96) and selective associations between humidity and acoustic features (r = 0.65 to 0.70), while thermal, acoustic, and behavioural domains remained largely independent. This pilot establishes baseline multimodal developmental patterns and supports parallel sensing for welfare-relevant monitoring in precision poultry farming.

### [48] [UniMamba: A Unified Spatial-Temporal Modeling Framework with State-Space and Attention Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16325)
*Xingsheng Chen,Xianpei Mu,Deyu Yi,Yilin Yuan,Xingwei He,Bo Gao,Regina Zhang,Pietro Lio,Siu-Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: UniMamba是一个统一的空间-时间预测框架，结合了高效的状态空间动态和基于注意力的依赖学习，用于多元时间序列预测，在准确性和计算效率上均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多元时间序列预测在能源、金融、环境监测等领域至关重要，但现有方法存在局限性：基于Transformer的方法能捕捉时间相关性但计算成本高（二次复杂度），而状态空间模型如Mamba虽然能高效建模长上下文但缺乏显式的时间模式识别能力。

Method: UniMamba框架包含三个核心组件：1) Mamba变体-通道编码层，结合FFT-Laplace变换和TCN来捕捉全局时间依赖；2) 空间-时间注意力层，联合建模变量间相关性和时间演化；3) 前馈时间动态层，融合连续和离散上下文进行准确预测。

Result: 在八个公共基准数据集上的综合实验表明，UniMamba在预测准确性和计算效率方面一致优于最先进的预测模型，为长序列多元时间序列预测提供了可扩展且稳健的解决方案。

Conclusion: UniMamba成功整合了高效状态空间动态和注意力依赖学习的优势，解决了现有方法的局限性，为多元时间序列预测提供了一个高效且准确的统一框架。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting is fundamental to numerous domains such as energy, finance, and environmental monitoring, where complex temporal dependencies and cross-variable interactions pose enduring challenges. Existing Transformer-based methods capture temporal correlations through attention mechanisms but suffer from quadratic computational cost, while state-space models like Mamba achieve efficient long-context modeling yet lack explicit temporal pattern recognition. Therefore we introduce UniMamba, a unified spatial-temporal forecasting framework that integrates efficient state-space dynamics with attention-based dependency learning. UniMamba employs a Mamba Variate-Channel Encoding Layer enhanced with FFT-Laplace Transform and TCN to capture global temporal dependencies, and a Spatial Temporal Attention Layer to jointly model inter-variate correlations and temporal evolution. A Feedforward Temporal Dynamics Layer further fuses continuous and discrete contexts for accurate forecasting. Comprehensive experiments on eight public benchmark datasets demonstrate that UniMamba consistently outperforms state-of-the-art forecasting models in both forecasting accuracy and computational efficiency, establishing a scalable and robust solution for long-sequence multivariate time-series prediction.

### [49] [Annotation Entropy Predicts Per-Example Learning Dynamics in LoRA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16332)
*Brady Steele*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: LoRA微调在标注分歧高的样本上表现出独特的"反学习"模式，这与全参数微调不同，揭示了参数高效微调方法处理有争议数据时的特殊行为

Abstract: We find that LoRA fine-tuning exhibits un-learning on contested examples: items with high annotator disagreement show increasing loss during training, a qualitatively distinct pattern largely absent under full fine-tuning and consistent across all six models tested (four encoder, two decoder-only). This discovery emerges from correlating annotation entropy, computed from ChaosNLI's 100 labels per example, with per-example area under the loss curve (AULC) on SNLI and MNLI. The correlation is positive in all 25 conditions tested (Spearman $ρ= 0.06$-$0.43$), with decoder-only models showing stronger correlations than encoders at matched LoRA rank. The effect survives partial-correlation controls and replicates across seeds and datasets. A preliminary noise-injection experiment is consistent with these findings.

*Pegah Ahadian,Mingrui Yang,Sixu Chen,Xiaojuan Li,Qiang Guan*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Knee osteoarthritis frequently exhibits discordance between structural damage observed in imaging and patient-reported symptoms such as pain. This mismatch complicates clinical interpretation and patient stratification and remains insufficiently modeled in existing decision support systems. We propose a discordance aware multimodal framework that combines machine learning prediction models with a tool grounded multi agent reasoning system. Using baseline data from the FNIH Osteoarthritis Biomarkers Consortium, we trained multimodal models to predict two progression tasks, joint space loss only progression versus non progression, and pain only progression versus non progression. The predictive system integrates three modality specific experts: a CatBoost tabular model using demographic, radiographic, MRI-derived scalar, and biomarker features; MRI image embeddings extracted using a ResNet18 backbone; and Xray embeddings derived from the same architecture. Expert predictions are fused using a stacking ensemble. Residual based models estimate expected pain from structural features, enabling the computation of a pain structure discordance score between observed and expected symptoms.
